msg:After visiting the original pulp center, I drove for half an hour to reach the hotel. There is a parking lot on the ground.
The hotel staff contacted me in advance to ask what time to arrive and other matters, saying that the room and children's supplies were prepared in advance. When checking in, I didn't feel that the room was prepared in advance. It was just arranged on the first floor according to the notes. I made a mistake and changed it twice. When I booked, I confirmed the upgraded room type, but I didn't take the initiative to ask when checking in. Later, I asked and said that it was arranged on the first floor. There was no upgraded room and no children's supplies. Later, I sent fruit.
There are many elevators, but you need to squeeze a little during peak hours. The lobby is very grand, the room is also spacious, and the basic facilities are complete. The TV is a little small, and there is less drinking water. The Internet speed is fast, there is a bathtub, the toiletries are very convenient, and the bed is comfortable. It is inevitable to encounter weddings and check-in during the festival, and it is noisy to knock on the door in the morning.
The breakfast variety is rich, the service is enthusiastic, and the noodle stall can cook vegetables and hot and sour noodles alone.
There is a small children's entertainment area. You can freeze your own things in the restaurant, and you need to sign an agreement, which is quite convenient. The hotel is a few steps away from Jin Street and the mall, which is very convenient for shopping and eating, especially at night. The overall stay was good and it was very quiet at night. I hope they will pay more attention to details.

msg:During the May Day holiday, I came to Tai'an to play and stayed at Tai'an R&F Wanda Realm Hotel for 3 consecutive days. It was very convenient to check in. We stayed in a deluxe suite. Our room was arranged on the 37th floor. The view was very good and we could see Mount Tai from a distance. At night, we could also see the lights on the top of Mount Tai. Wanda Mall and Golden Street were downstairs, which made it very convenient for eating and shopping. The branch of Little Goat BBQ was also downstairs, and it was only a 200-meter walk away. There were also a series of Tai'an snacks such as braised pork, etc. You didn't need to drive to go around the city. There were shared electric bicycles downstairs, which were very convenient to ride out. It was only a few kilometers away from the night market of Dai Temple.
The water quality of the hotel's swimming pool was relatively clear. We swam twice in the 3-day stay. It was mainly because we couldn't do this kind of physical activity after climbing Mount Tai, so we soaked in the water for a while.
The hotel's breakfast is quite rich, the hot and sour noodles are delicious, and the chives dumplings are also delicious. I stayed for 3 days and didn't eat them for the first two days. On the last day, I saw chive dumplings and quickly took 2 pieces. In the end, an uncle cleared them all... The breakfast manager Zhao was warm and thoughtful, and also gave children breakfast. I was very satisfied.
I love this small city of Tai'an so much. I will stay here for a few days if I have the chance.
